\bentry
\word[each(1)]{each}
\pron{Icf}
\gl{\gu}
{\dictmeaning{(eraDu yA hecicxnavugaLa naDuve biDibiDiyAgi
parigaNisida) parxti; 
parxtiyoMdara; parxtiyobabxna(La); oMdoMdara; obobxbabxna(La): 
\eng{each man has two votes} parxtiyobabxnigU eraDu OTugaLive. 
\eng{we have two votes each} namamxlilx parxtiyobabxnigU eraDu OTugaLive. 
\eng{each is worse than the one before} parxtiyoMdU adara hiMdinadakikxMta keTaTxdAgide.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\eng{each and every} oMdoMdU; parxtiyoMdU.}
\eentry

\bentry

javAbAgiruva BujagaLu oMdakokxMdu samavAgive.}}

\noindent

inonxbabxnanunx yA obabxLu inonxbabxLanunx: \eng{they hate each other} avaru 
parasapxra devxVSisutAtxre; parxtiyobabxnU uLidavaranunx devxVSisutAtxne.
\eng{they wore each other's hats} avaru parasapxra ToVpigaLanunx hAkikoMDaru; 
avaralilx obobxbabxnU inonxbabxna ToVpiyanunx hAkikoMDa.

modala (\birx) mUru yA (\ame) eraDu sAthxnagaLalilx baruvudeMdu bAji
kaTuTxvudu.}

\bentry
\word[ear(1)]{ear}
\pron{iarf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num {1} kivi; kaNaR; shoVrxtarx; sharxvaNeVMdirxya (\kanmu\ horaBAga). 
\num{2} sharxvaNa shakitx; shabadxgarxhaNashakitx; nAdajAcnxna; nAda 
saMveVdane: \eng{an ear for music} saMgiVtakekx kivi; saMgiVtajAcnxna. 
\num{3} 
sharxvaNa; keVLemx; keVLuvike. 
\num{4} gamana; lakaSxyX. 
\num{5} kiviyAkArada 
vasutx, \kanmu\ hUjiya hiDi.}}

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{a word in your ears} kivimAtu; guTuTxmAtu; pisumAtu; 
kiviyalilx, guTATxgi, aMtaraMgadalilx --- oMdu mAtu. 
\num{2} \eng{be all ears} 
meYyelAlx kiviyAgiru; manasisxTuTx Alisu; kivigoTuTx keVLu. 
\num{3} \eng{bring (storm, hornet's nest, etc.) about one's ears} birugALi meVleraguvaMte mADiko;
kaNajagaLanunx ebibxsi ilalxda PajiVti, toMdare mADiko; ilalxda apAya meYmeVle 
taMduko. 
\num{4} \eng{ears \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{burn(2) nuga(11)}{${}^2$burn}.} 
\num{5} \eng{ear to the ground} gALisudidx yA
aBipArxyagaLa olavina bagege ecacxrike yA jAgarUkate. 
\num{6} \eng{give ear} kivigoDu; Alisi 
keVLu; manasisxTuTx, gamanaviTuTx -- keVLu. 
\num{7} \eng{give one's ears} (yAvudeV vasutxvige, 
yAvudaneVnx mADalu) yAvudeV tAyxgavanAnxdarU mADu: \eng{I would give my ears}
(oMdu kAyaRkAkxgi, vasutxvigAgi) Enu beVkAdarU koTeTxVnu; eSuTx
tAyxgavanAnxdarU 
mADiyeVnu. 
\num{8} \eng{have person's ear} obabxna pirxVti, vishAvxsa, naMbike,
anugarxha --- saMpAdisu: \eng{he has his master's ear} avanu heVLidaMte avana 
yajamAna keVLutAtxne; yajamAnana kivi avana keYyalilxde. 
\num{9} \eng{head over ears = \hyperlink{ear(1)nuga12}{\nuga $(12)$}}. 
\num{10} \eng{in (at) one ear and out (at) the other}
oMdu kiviyanunx hokukx inonxMdu kiviyalilx hoVgutatxde; yAva parimANavanUnx 
uMTumADuvudilalx. 
\num{11} \eng{out on one's ear} apamAnakaravAgi 
tirasakxrisida yA kaDegaNisida. 
\hypertarget{ear(1)nuga12}{}
\num{12} \eng{over head and ears} (sAla, 
perxVma, \mo vugaLalilx) iLiya muLugi; pUtiR muLugi: \eng{over head and ears in
debt} meYyelAlx sAladalilx muLugi. 
\num{13} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_p.pdf}{P}{play(1) pagu(9)}{${}^1$play}
by ear}.    
\num{14} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_p.pdf}{P}{prick(2)
pagu(3)}{${}^2$prick} up one's ear }. 
\num{15} \eng{set (persons) by the ears} tarale 
ebibxsu; (janaralilx) manasAtxpa huTiTxsu; kitApati mADu; kitAtxTa hacucx; jagaLa huTiTxsu. 
\num{16} \eng{to be set by the ears}
manasAtxpakekx oLagAgi. 
\num{17} \eng{turn a \hyperref{kandict_d.pdf}{D}{deaf pagu(4)}{deaf} ear}. 
\num{18} \eng{up to the
ears} (\AmA) kiviyavaregU muLugi; (oLasaMcu, sAla, kelasa, \mo vugaLalilx) 
bahaLa ALavAgi sikikxhAkikoMDu yA muLugi. 
\num{19} \eng{wet behind the ears} 
apakavxvAda; ananuBaviyAda; anuBavavilalxda. 
\num{20} \eng{with a \hyperref{kandict_f.pdf}{F}{flea nuga}{flea} in
his ear}.}}

\num{3} \eng{eat its head off} (kudure \mo\ 
pArxNigaLa \vi) Aguva parxyoVjanakikxMta tiMDi tiVni vecacx hecucx; lABakikxMta
KacuR vecacx hecAcxgiru; hAgada koVLi mupApxgada kALu tiMditu. 
\num{4} \eng{eat one's
dinners}= \hyperlink{eat nuga(6)}{\nuga {\rm (6)}.} 
\num{5} \eng{eat one's heart out} manasisxge 
hacicxkoMDu atiyAgi koragutitxru, sadA vayxthepaDutitxru. 
\hyperdef{E}{eat nuga(6)}{} \hypertarget{eat nuga(6)}{}
\num{6} \eng{eat 
one's terms} (\birx) vakilavqtitxgAgi Odu, vAyxsaMga mADu (matutx adakAkxgi 
infsxAphf koVTiRnalilx nigadita sala UTamADu). 
\hyperdef{E}{eat nuga(7)}{} 
\num{7} \eng{eat one's words} 
ADida mAtanunx (avamAnakara riVtiyalilx) hiMtegeduko, nuMgiko; tanagAguva 
avamAnavanunx nuMgikoMDu hiMde ADidadx mAtanunx vApasusx tegeduko. 
\num{8} \eng{eat out of person's hand} (obabxnige) saMpURNa adhiVnavAgiru; pUtiR 
vashavatiRyAgiru; inonxbabxna keY tututx tinunx. 
\num{9} \eng{eat (person) out
of house and home} manemAranenxlAlx tiMdu hAki (vayxkitxyanunx) nAshamADu; 
tiMdu tiMdu (obabxna) mane hALu mADu.
\num{10} \eng{well, don't eat me} (tiVvarxvAgi edurADutitxruvavanige
yA joVrAgi parxtivAda mADutitxruvavanige utatxravAgi) noVDu noVDu,
nananx tiMduhAkabeVDa; ayAyx, nananxnunx tinanxbeVDa. 
\num{11} \eng{what's eating you?} (\AmA) ninanxnunx Enu tinunxtitxde? 
ninanxnunx kADutitxruvudeVnu? Eke kirikiri paDutitxdidxVye?}
\eentry

\bentry

{\dictmeaning{

soVpAnapaMkitx; parasapxra samAnAMtaravAgi matutx seYnikadaLagaLanunx

(\kanmu\ haDagugaLu).

parxdhAna viBAga. 
\num{4} adhikAravagaR; yAvudeV saMsethxyalilx yA saMGadalilx 
oMdeV aMtasutx yA vagaRkekx seVrida vayxkitxgaLu: \eng{the higher echelons of

\bentry

\num{3} (parxsidadhx kavi, BAva, BAvane, sheYli, \mo vugaLa) gADha anukaraNa; 
hatitxrada hoVlike; samIpasAmayx: \eng{containing strong echoes from Milton} 
milaTxnanxna kAvayxda anukaraNaviruva, hatitxrada hoVlike iruva.

anukaraNaka; anukaraNakAri; anukaraNe mADuvavanu; anukarisuvavanu. 
\num{5} 
aMtAyxkaSxri; oMdu pAdada aMtAyxkaSxragaLanunx muMdina pAdada yA muMdina 
payARya pAdada AdayxkaSxragaLanAnxgi baLasuva camatAkxra. 
\hyperdef{E}{echo(1)6}{}
\num{6} (birxjf yA 
visfTx ATadalilx tananx jotegAranu turupu \mo vanunx ADi niVDida sUcanege 
parxtiyAgi tAnU adanenxV ADi toVrisuva) parxtisUcane. 
\num{7} vqtatxpatirxke;

\num{8} 
parxtiPalita (reVDiyoV yA reVDArf) taraMga. 
\num{9} PalitAMsha; pariNAma; 
Palashurxti; parxtikirxye: \eng{the economic collapse had dangerous political
echoes} A AthiRka kusitadiMdAgi apAyakara rAjakiVya parxtikirxyegaLuMTAdavu.}}

vayxMgayx.

beTaTxguDaDx yA dibabxda netitx) 
\num{5} (oMdu GanAkaqtiya eraDu muKagaLu seVruva) ENu; aMcu. 
\num{6} (oMdu teLu 
vasutxvina hora meYya) aMcu; tudi. 
\num{7} (parxpAtada) arugu; tudi; ENu; aMcu.
\num{8} (oMdu parxdeVshada yA meVlemxYya) elelx gere; siVmAreVKe; gaDireVKe.}}

\num{1} \eng{bad egg} (\ashi)

\alnum{a} aparxyoVjaka vayxkitx; ayoVgayx AsAmi.

\alnum{b} moVsagAra. 

\alnum{c} goDuDx yoVjane, haMcike; niSaPxlavAguva 
yoVjane; vayxthaR haMcike. 
\num{2} \eng{good eggs} (\ashi) 

\alnum{a} oLeLxya AsAmi; yoVgayx. 

\alnum{b} oLeLxya vasutx. 

\alnum{c} (aBinaMdanAsUcakavAgi) Bale; 
BeVSf; shABAsf. 
\num{3} \eng{have all one's eggs in one basket} tananx 
samasatxvanUnx oMdeV sAhasa, udayxma yA parxyatanxdalilx paNavAgisu, hUDu, 
toDagisu, oDuDx. 
\num{4} \eng{in the egg}

\alnum{a} moLakeyalilx; pArxraMBa deseyalilx. 

\alnum{b} inUnx beLeyada, vikasisada. 
\num{5} \eng{teach one's 
grandmother to suck eggs} ajijxge kemamxlu heVLikoDu; ajajxnige aMbegAliDalu 
kalisu; tanagiMta hecucx anuBavige budidhxvAda heVLu. 
\num{6} \eng{with egg on
one's face} (\AmA) daDaDx kaLeyiMda; pedudx kaLeyiMda.}

\bentry
\word[eight(1)]{eight}
\pron{ETf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} eMTu; aSaTx. 
\num{2} eMTara cihenx (\eng{8, viii,
VIII}). 
\num{3} (sekxVTiMgf ATadalilx) oMdanonxMdu otitxkoMDu $8$ra
AkAradalilxruva eraDu vqtatxgaLu. 
\num{4} aSaTxka; eMTu janara yA
vasutxgaLa yA GaTakagaLa oMdu taMDa, seTuTx: \eng{crew of eight in
rowing boat} (doVNi naDesuvalilx) eMTu jana cAlakara taMDa. 
\num{5}
(isipxVTu) eMTara ele; eMTu boTuTxgaLa gurutiruva isipxVTele. 
\hypertarget{eight(1)6}{}
\num{6}
`$8$'ra AkArada citarx, Akqti. 
\num{7} eMTu gaMTe; eMTara
samaya.

gAtarx \mo vu.

\bentry
\word{electricity}
\pron{i(e)lekiTxrXsiTi}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} viduyxtutx; yAvudeV vasutxvayxvasethxyalilx ilekATxrXnugaLa
hecacxLa yA korateya kAraNa, karxmavAgi QuNa matutx dhana eMba eraDu bageyalilx
meYdoVruva oMdu bageya Bwta asitxtavx. 
\num{2} viduyxtf parxvAha; diVpa \mo 
vugaLige viduyxtf pUreYke. 
\num{3} viduyxtf shAsatxrX; viduyxtitxge 
saMbaMdhisida shAsatxrX.}}

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{frictional electricity} GaSaRNe viduyxtutx; padAthaRgaLa
naDuvaNa GaSaRNeyiMda uMTAguva viduyxtutx. 
\num{2} \eng{galvanic electricity}
gAyxlavxnika viduyxtutx; rAsAyanika kirxyeyiMda utapxtitxyAda viduyxtutx.
\num{3} \eng{magnetic electricity} kAMtatA viduyxtutx; kAMtateyiMda 
utapxtitxyAda viduyxtutx. 
\num{4} \eng{resinous electricity} rALa viduyxtutx;
rALadalilx utapxtitxmADida viduyxtutx. 
\num{5} \eng{static electricity} 
sithxtividuyxtutx; hariyade oMdu sathxLakekx siVmitavAgiruva viduyxtutx. 
\num{6} \eng{thermal electricity} uSaNx viduyxtutx; 
uSaNxdiMda utapxtitxyAda viduyxtutx. 
\num{7} \eng{vitreous electricity} gAju
viduyxtutx; gAjinalilx utapxtitx mADida viduyxtutx.}
\eentry

(kaNuNx, dhavxni, Ase, Baravase, \mo vugaLa) Erike; etatxrisike; utAthxna.

\num{5} (baMdUkina yA PiraMgiya) akaSxvanunx etatxrisuvudu. 
\num{6} (aMtasutx,
dajeR \mo vugaLa) Erike; aunanxtayx. 
\num{7} (guri, dheyxVya, udedxVsha, 
sheYli, \mo vugaLa) utatxmike; utakxSaRNe. 
\num{8} unanxti; (\kanmu\ 
baMdUka yA AkAshakAyada dikikxna \vi) baMdUkakUkx kiSxtijiVya reVKegU iruva 
koVna. 
\num{9} (oMdu nidiRSaTx maTaTxda meVlina, \kanmu\ samudarxmaTaTxda 
meVlina) etatxra; unanxti. 
\num{10} unanxti; UdhavxR samatalada meVle mADuva 
kaTaTxDada Akqti yA nakeSx; mane \mo vugaLa pakakx, muMBAga, hiMBAgagaLanunx 
toVrisuva capapxTe nakAse. 
\num{11} unanxti; aunanxtayx; veYBava; ucACxrXya; 
utakxSaR; Ganate; meVlemx. 
\num{12} etatxravAda sathxLa; unanxta sathxLa. 

\num{13} (bAyxle) negeta; sAnxyugaLanunx bigigoLisi iDiV shariVravanunx 
neladiMda meVlakekxVrisuva negeta.}

biDisu; baMdhana tapipxsu; biDugaDemADu; vimoVcanegoLisu. 
\num{3} (gulAmananunx)

vimoVcanegoMDa vayxkitxgaLu; vimukatx vayxkitxgaLu.}

\pron{eMbirxO}
\gl{\nA} (\bava\ \eng{embryos}).
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} BUrxNa; (gaBaR)piMDa; moTeTxyiMda yA 
gaBaRdiMda horabaruvudakekx muMcina sithxtiyalilxruva pArxNi. 
\num{2} 
BUrxNAMkura; mAnavagaBaRdalilxruva, gaBaRdhAraNeyiMda eMTu vAragaLoLagina 
BUrxNa. 
\num{3} pArxraMBada yA mUlarUpadalilxruva vasutx. 
\num{4} mUlarUpa; 
AraMBasithxti; apakavxrUpa. 
\num{5} (\savi) moLake; muMgu; aMkura; inUnx 
biVjadalelxV iruva giDada mUlarUpa.}}

sithxti, \mo vugaLiMda) pArAgu; biDugaDe hoMdu; horabaru: \eng{the common 
people emerged from illiteracy} sAmAnayx jana anakaSxrateyiMda pArAdaru. 
\num{4} (saMgati \mo vugaLa \vi) horapaDu; bayalAgu; tiLidubaru;
vayxkatxvAgu; beLakige

\bentry
\word[en-(1)]{en-}
\pron{enf-, inf-}
\gl{\pUparx}
\dictmeaning{(= \eng{\hyperref{kandict_i.pdf}{I}{in-(1)}{${}^1$in-}})
kirxyApadagaLanunx racisalu baLasuva \pUparx: 

\alnum{a} `oMdu vasutxvanunx inonxMdara oLage yA oLakekx' eMba athaRdalilx \nA gaLiMda 
\kirx gaLanunx racisuva \pUparx: \eng{embed, engulf.} 

\alnum{b} `oMdu 
vasutxvanoVnx viSayavanonxV oMdara yA obabxna vashakekx' eMbathaRdalilx \nA 
gaLiMda \kirx gaLanunx racisuva \pUparx: \eng{entrust.} 

\alnum{c} \nA gaLiMdaloV
\gu gaLiMdaloV `oMdu sithxtige taru' eMba athaRda \kirx gaLanunx racisuva 
\pUparx: \eng{enable, enslave,} halavu veVLe \eng{-en} \uparx doDane,
\udA\ 
\eng{embolden, enlighten}. 

\alnum{d} \kirx gaLiMda `oLakekx' yA meVle' eMbathaRda
\kirx gaLanunx racisuvAga baLasuva \pUparx: \eng{enfold}. 

\alnum{e} \kirx 
gaLalilx utakxSaRkAthaR sUcisalu baLasuva \pUparx\ \eng{encarnalize}.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[end(1)]{end}
\pron{eMDf}
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} kone; tudi; miti; meVre; elelx: \eng{there is no end to it}
adakekx koneyilalx. 
\num{2} aMtayx; aMta; kaDe; tudi; kone: \eng{end of a line}
reVKeya (sAlina) tudi, kone. 
\num{3} (yAvudeV vasutxvina) oMdu kaDeya tudi; A 
kaDeya yA I kaDeya tudi. 
\num{4} uLike; tuMDu; moVTu; avasheVSa; uLidadudx: 
\eng{candle ends} meVNada batitxya (uridu mikakx) tuMDugaLu. 
\num{5} (kAla, 
kAyaR, sithxti, garxMtha, \mo vugaLa) kone; aMtayx; mukAtxya; samApitx; mugivu;
mugita. 
\num{6} kone; aMtayx; kaDegAla; konegAla; aMtima sithxti: \eng{in the 
end of autumn} sharadaqtuvina konegAladalilx. 
\num{7} kone; aMtayx; aLivu; 
nAsha; hALu: \eng{the end of civilisation} nAgarikateya kone, nAsha. 
\num{8} maraNa; sAvu; kone; aMtayx. 
\num{9} parxyoVjana; Pala; udedxVsha; upayoVga; 
PalitAMsha: \eng{to what end}? yAva parxyoVjanakAkxgi? \eng{to gain his ends}
avana udedxVshasAdhanegAgi. 
\num{10} (yAvudeV oMdara asitxtavxda) guri; 
udedxVsha; aMtima, niNARyaka kAraNa: \eng{the happiness of the people is the 
end of government} janara saMtoVSaveV sakARrada guri. 
\num{11} (atayxMta 
dUrada) biMdu; tudi; kone: \eng{to the ends of the earth} BUmiya tudiyavaregU.
\num{12} kaDe; BAga; tudi; kone: \eng{no problem at my end} nananx kaDe yAva 
samaseyxyU ilalx. 
\num{13} oMdu taMDa yA obabx ATagAra AkarxmisikoMDiruva 
kirxVDAMgaNada yA ATada meYdAnada adhaRBAga, pakakx. 
\num{14} (\ame, kenaDa) 
sAlina yA taMDada koneyalilxruva phuTfbAlf ATagAra. 
\num{15} (boVlf\char 144 ATa) hulilxna ATada meYdAnada oMdu tudiyiMda
inonxMdu tudiyavarege ADuva ATada oMdu GaTaka.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{deep end} IjukoLadalilx niVru ALavAgiruva tudi yA BAga; 
ALavAda kone, pakakx. 
\num{2} \eng{end for end} tudiya sAthxnagaLanunx 
badalAyisuvaMte, adalubadalu mADuvaMte; talekeLakAgi. 
\num{3} \eng{end on} 

\alnum{a} (kaNiNxge) tudi edurAgi; yAvudAdarU vasutxvina tudiyu noVDuvavara 
kaNiNxge neVravAgi tirugi niMtiruvaMte yA adu inonxMdu vasutxvige 
neVravAgiruvaMte. 

\alnum{b} tuditudi kUDi; muMdina vasutxvina tudige kUDikoMDu.
\num{4} \eng{end to end} udadxkUkx; ududxdadxkekx niraMtaravAgi; tudiyiMda 
tudige: \eng{placed end to end} ududxdadxvAgi kone kone kUDisi iTaTx; 
tuditudigUDisida. 
\num{5} \eng{rope's end} (cATiyiMda) hoDeyalu kaseya 
tudiyalilx dAradiMda kaTiTxda saNaNx gaMTu. 
\num{6} \eng{shoemaker's end} 
moVcihuri; meVNa hAki hurimADida birugUdalina koneyuLaLx moVciyavana dAra.}}

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{all ends up} saMpUNaRvAgi; pUtiRyAgi. 
\num{2} \eng{at a loose end} kelasavilalxde; anishicxta sithxtiyalilx: \eng{he spent two years wandering about the country at a loose end} Ata EnU kelasavilalxde deVshadalilx
aledADutatx eraDu vaSaR kaLeda. 
\num{3} \eng{at an end} mugiduhoVgi; 
koneyalilx. 
\num{4} \eng{at one's wits (\engit{or} wit's) end} EnU toVcade; 
digaBxrXmeyAgi; hiMdumuMdu toVrade; kakAkxbikikxyAgi. 
\hypertarget{end1 nuga5}{}
\num{5} \eng{be at an end}
 
\alnum{a} mugiduhoVgu; mukAtxyavAgu; konegoLuLx; tudimuTuTx; konetalupu;
pUtiRyAgu: \eng{the meeting was at an end} saBe mukAtxyavAyitu. 

\alnum{b} baLaliru; susAtxgiru; AyAsagoMDiru. 
\num{6} \eng{be at the end of one's tether}
jANemx, sahane, shakitx, \mo vugaLelalx tiVrihoVgi: \eng{a succession of 
illness had brought him to the end of his tether} kAyilegaLa paraMpareyiMda 
avana shakitxyelalxvU tiVriyeVhoVgitutx. 
\num{7} \eng{come to a bad end} 

\alnum{a} nAshavAgu; hAnigoLagAgu.
 
\alnum{b} avamAnakokxLagAgu; agwravakekx guriyAgu;
tananx tapupxgaLiMda hAni, kaLaMka, shikeSx, \mo vugaLige oLagAgu. 
\num{8} \eng{come to an end} = \hyperlink{end1 nuga5}{\nuga $(5)$}. 
\num{9} \eng{draw to an end} mugi; kone 
muTuTx. 
\num{10} \eng{end of the road} koneya sAthxnadalilx; kaTaTxkaDeya 
sathxLadalilx; baduku \mo vu sAdhayxveV ilalxdaMtha sAthxnadalilx, 
sithxtiyalilx. 
\num{11} \eng{get hold of the wrong end of the stick} (athaR yA 
udedxVshavanunx) tapApxgi garxhisu. 
\num{12} \eng{go (in) off the deep end}

\alnum{a} (sAkxcf IjukaTeTxya \vi) apAya lakiSxsade mununxgugx; naSaTxkekx 
sidadhxnAgiru. 

\alnum{b} (\AmA) (anAvashayxkavAgi) kaLavaLapaDu; udivxganxgAgu;
udevxVgakokxLagAgu; gAbariyAgu; manaHsethxYyaR kaLeduko: \eng{she goes off the 
deep end at the mention of his name} avana hesaru heVLidare sAku, avaLu 
udivxganxLAgutAtxLe. 

\alnum{c} (\AmA) siTATxgu; koVpakoLuLx. 

\alnum{d} vipariVtakekx hoVgu; mitimIru: \eng{he certainly went off
the deep end with that last idea} avana kaTaTxkaDeya yoVcane
noVDidare, avanu vipariVtakekx hoVgidAdxne aninxsutatxde. 
\num{13} \eng{have at one's finger's end} karagata
mADikoMDiru; sidadhxvAgiTuTxkoMDiru. 
\num{14} \eng{in the end} konege; 
kaTaTxkaDeyalilx; AKeYrAgi. 
\hyperdef{E}{end(1) nuga(15)}{}
\num{15} \eng{keep one's end up} 

\alnum{a} (vAyxpAra
\mo vugaLalilx) dakaSxteyiMda tananx pAlina kelasa nivaRhisu. 

\alnum{b} (saMBASaNe, ATa, \mo vugaLalilx) tananx pAtarxvanunx
yashasivxyAgi vahisu. 
\num{16} \eng{make an end of} sAkumADu; nililxsu; mugisu; konegANisu.
\hyperdef{E}{end(1) nuga(17)}{} \hypertarget{end(1) nuga(17)}{}
\num{17} \eng{make both ends meet} varamAnavanUnx vecacxvanUnx
sarihoMdisu; tanage 
baruvaSuTx varamAnadalilx kAlahAku; AdAya vecacx saritUguvaMte jiVvana
naDesu. 
\num{18} \eng{make ends meet} = \hyperlink{end(1) nuga(17)}{\nuga $(17)$}. 
\num{19} \eng{no end} (\AmA) 
bahaLa; apAra; atayxMta; bahaLaSuTx: \eng{they were pleased no end by the warm

\num{20} \eng{no end of} (\AmA) 

\alnum{a} bahaLa; sAkaSuTx. 

\alnum{b} halavAru; aneVka.

\alnum{a} eDebiDade; oMdeV samanAgi;

\alnum{b} neTaTxge; neVravAgi (iDu, nililxsu): \eng{place the drum on end}

\alnum{b} nAshamADu; hALumADu.

guMDu avananunx mugisitu. 
\num{3} pUrayisu; mugisu; mukAtxyagoLisu: \eng{he
ended his drudging labour} beVsara taruva tananx duDimeyanunx avanu 
mukAtxyagoLisida.}}

\noindent 
\gl{\akirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} konegANu; mugi; tiVrihoVgu. 
\num{2} payaRvasAnavAgu; 
samApatxvAgu; pariNAmagoLuLx: \eng{extravagance ends in want} duMdugArike 
aBAvadalilx payaRvasAnagoLuLxtatxde.}}

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{end by doing} konege mADibiDu; aMtimavAgi mADibiDu: 
\eng{will end by marrying a duke} konege obabx DUyxkananunx 
maduveyAgibiDutAtxLe. 
\num{2} \eng{end in} PalavAgu; pariNAmavAgu: \eng{the 
scheme ended in failure} yoVjane niSaPxlavAyitu. 
\num{3} \eng{end it (all)}
(\AmA) Atamxhateyx mADiko; tananxnenxV konegoLisu; jiVva tegeduko. 
\num{4} \eng{end off} mugisu; mukAtxyagoLisu: \eng{he ended off his
speech wth some jokes} avanu kelavu hAsayx caTAkigaLiMda tananx BASaNa
mugisida. 
\num{5} 
\eng{end up} koneyAgu; mugi; mukAtxyavAgu; guri talupu: \eng{he ended up in the
jail} konege avanu jeYluseVrida.}

\bentry

\gl{\nA}

vasutx.}}

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
{\dictmeaning{\eng{the Enemy} seYtAna; pApadeVvate.}}

\noindent 
\gl{\nuga}
\dictmeaning{
\hypertarget{enemy1 nuga1}{}
\num{1} \eng{be nobody's enemy but one's own} tananx duradaqSaTxkekx,
vinAshakekx tAneV javabAdxranAgu; tanage tAneV hageyAgu; savxyaMshaturxvAgu.

\word{epicure}
\pron{epikuyxarf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} rasika; suKaBoVgi; rasajacnx; rucigAra; tinunxvudu, 
kuDiyuvudu, sAhitayx, \mo vugaLalilx utatxmavAdudanUnx ruciyAdudanUnx 
saviyuvavanu. 
\num{2} BoVgalAlasa; iMdirxyasuKAsakatx; viSayAsakatx.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[epicurean(1)]{epicurean}
\pron{epikuyxari(V)anf}
\gl{\gu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (\eng{Epicurean}) epikUyxrasana; \kirxpU $4$neV shatamAnada
girxVkf tatatxvXjAcnxni epikUyxrasfna sidAdhxMtakekx saMbaMdhapaTaTx. 
\num{2} 
rasika; suKAsakatx; suKapirxya; utatxmABiruciyuLaLx; sUkASxmXBiruciyuLaLx; 
(\kanmu\ nAjUkAda) iMdirxya suKAnuBoVgadalilx anurakatxnAda: \eng{an epicurean
family} rasika manetana. 
\num{3} roVcaka; iMdirxyagaLanunx uderxVkisuva hAgU
taqpitxgoLisuva: \eng{epicurean dishes} nAligeyanunx taqpitxgoLisuvaMtha 
BakaSxyXgaLu. 
\num{4} BoVgiya; BoVgAsakatxna; viSayAsakatxna; 
BoVgaparxvaqtitxya jiVvana.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[epicurean(2)]{epicurean}
\pron{epikuyxari(V)anf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} epikUyxriyanf; parama oLitu iruvudu saMtoVSadalilx aMdare 
sadAcAradalilx eMdu boVdhisida \kirxpU $4$neV shatamAnada athenisxna 
tatatxvXjAcnxni epikUyxrasasxna anuyAyi. 
\num{2} rasika; BoVgi; BoVgAsakatx;
suKaloVla; suKapirxya; (\kanmu\ unanxtamaTaTxda) iMdirxya suKAnuBoVgadalilx 
anurakatxnAdavanu.}

\bentry
\word{epicycle}
\pron{episeYkflf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (\jAyx) adhicakarx; episeYkalf; doDaDx vaqtatxvoMdara 
paridhiya meVle uruLuva oMdu saNaNxvaqtatx. 
\num{2} (\Kavi) adhicakarx; (TAlemi
sidAdhxMtada parxkAra) oMdu doDaDx vaqtatxda paridhiya meVle calisuva 
keVMdarxvuLaLx cikakxdoMdu vaqtatx (I cikakx vaqtatxda paridhiya meVle garxha 
calisuvudeMbudu sidAdhxMta).}

\bentry
\word{epiphany}
\pron{i(e)piphani}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (\eng{Epiphany}) meVjeY eMba pwrasatxyX jAcnxnigaLige 
kirxsatxnu kANisikoMDadudx. 
\num{2} sAkASxtAkxra; deVvara parxtayxkaSx; 
atimAnuSa vayxkitxya parxtayxkaSx. 
\num{3} sAkASxtAkxra dina; kirxYsatxnu 
meVjeYgaLige kANisikoMDadadxra jAcnxpakAthaRvAgi kerxYsatxru janavari $6$neya
tAriVKu Acarisuva hababx. 
\num{4} aMtaboRVdhe; aMtajAcnxRna; oLaarivu; 
yAvudAdarU oMdu saraLa, sAmAnayx GaTaneya yA nitayx jiVvanada anuBavada mUlaka
idadxkikxdadxMte oMdu vasutxvina (agoVcara) satayxte yA jiVvanada vAsatxvateya 
bagege mUDuva oLa arivu. 
\num{5} aMtaboRVdhe; oLa arivu yA anuBavada 
sAkASxtAkxra mADikoDuva oMdu sAhitayxkaqti yA kaqtiya oMdu athaRpUNaR 
saninxveVsha yA BAga: \eng{the epiphany in ``Oedipus'', the final tableau of 
the blinded old man} `IDipasf' nATakada aMtaboRVdhajanaka saninxveVsha aMdare 
kaNuNx kuruDAgi baruva mudukana aMtima mUkadaqshayx.}
\eentry

\gl{\gu}

\bentry

\alnum{b} \gu gaLalilx: \eng{scaler,
lunar, solar}. 
\num{2} lAYxTinf BASeya \gu gaLalilx \eng{-arius} matutx

\num{3}

\eng{-eure} Agi iMgilxSfnalilx

huTiTxruva \nA gaLalilx: \eng{boarder, counter}. 

\alnum{b} \eng{-ure} rUpakekx

seVrida, tupupxLu camaRda, muMgusi jAtiya, mAMsAhAri
pArxNi. \quad\hyperlink{ermine-1figure}{\raisebox{-0.15cm}[0pt][0pt]{\pdfimage
    width 0.7cm height 0.5cm {E_Pictures/ermine-1.jpg}}}
\num{2} 
(nAyxyAdhiVshara matutx variSaThxvagaRdavara adhikArada kuruhAda 
niluvaMgigaLalilx baLasuva) amiRninxna biLi tupupxLu camaR. 
\num{3} gwrava 
hAgU parishudadhxteya saMkeVta.

biLi tupupxLu camaR.}

\bentry
\wordwithhyphen{hyp-ery}{-ery}
\pron{-ari}
\gl{\uparx}
\dictmeaning{muMde heVLuva athaRgaLanunxLaLx padagaLanunx racisuvAga baLasuva 
\uparx: 
\num{1} sarakugaLu; oMdu vagaRda sAmAnugaLu: \eng{drapery}. 
\num{2} 
oMdu vagaRkekx seVrisida vasutxgaLu: \eng{greenery, machinery}. 
\num{3} 
(janagaLa) guMpu; vagaR; samUha: \eng{citizenry}. 
\num{4} baLake yA sithxti: 
\eng{archery, dupery}. 
\num{5} kelasa, vayxvasAya, taLiya aBivaqdidhx --- ivugaLa,
(\ame) ivu doreyuva sathxLa: \eng{brewery, vinery, piggery}. 
\num{6} vataRne; 
naDate: \eng{foolery, mimicry}. 
\num{7} (hecAcxgi \tu) saMbaMdhapaTaTx elalxvU;
tatasxMbaMdhi: \eng{popery, Whiggery}. 
\num{8} (vasutxgaLa \vi) A bageya; A
rUpada; A guNada; A savxBAvada.}

\bentry
\word[escape(1)]{escape}
\pron{i(e)sekxVpf}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (nibaRMdha, apAya, \mo vugaLiMda) vimoVcane; biDugaDe; 
pArAguvudu; tapipxsikoLuLxvudu; tapipxsikoMDu hoVguvudu. 
\num{2} pArAda 
sithxti; pArAguvike; tapipxsikoLuLxvike: 
\eng{a narrow escape, 
hairbreadth escape} bahaLa savxlapx avakAshadalilx, kUdaleLeyaSaTxralilx --- 
tapipxsikoMDadudx, pArAdadudx. 
\num{3} pArAguva mAgaR, hAdi, sAdhana; apAya \mo 
vugaLiMda tapipxsikoLaLxlu sahAya mADuva sAdhana: \eng{we used the window as an
escape} nAvu kiTakiyanunx pArAguva sAdhanavAgi baLasidevu. 
\num{4} palAyana;
apakaSaRNe; yathAthaRteyiMda dUravAguvudu; vAsatxvika yA satayxsithxtiyiMda 
ODihoVgalu yA manasasxnunx beVreDege seLeyalu sahAyakavAguva \kanmu\ sAhitayx,
saMgiVta, \mo\ sAdhana: \eng{mythological stories can be an escape} pwrANika 
kathegaLu (vAsatxvikateyiMda) palAyanavAgabahudu. 
\num{5} (anila, niVru, \mo 
vu) soVrike; soVrihoVguvudu. 
\num{6} toVTada kaLe; kADusasiyaMte beLeyuva 
toVTada sasayx; tAneVtAnAgi habubxva toVTada giDa, kaLe. 
\num{7} pAreVNi; 
uripAru ENi (sAdhana); beMkihotitxkoMDa maneyiMda oLagiruvavaranunx rakiSxsalu
upayoVgisuva ENi, sAdhana.}
\eentry 

\bentry
\word[escape(2)]{escape}
\pron{i(e)sekxVpf}
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (manuSayx, hiDita, \mo vugaLiMda) jAriko; nusuLiko; 
tapipxsiko; nuNuciko: \eng{he escaped the police} avanu poVlisariMda 
tapipxsikoMDa. 
\num{2} (iSaTxvalalxdadxnunx, aniSaTxvAdudanunx) tore; tayxjisu;
biTuTxbiDu. 
\num{3} mare; nenapiniMda jArihoVgu; gamanakekx yA jAcnxpakakekx 
bAradiru; nenapiniMda nusuLihoVgu: \eng{his name had escaped me} avana hesaru 
nanage mareteVhoVgitutx. 
\num{4} (mAtu, niTuTxsiru, \mo vu bAyiyiMda) tapipx 
baMdubiDu; ayatanxvAgi horabiVLu; aparxyatanxvAgi horabaru. 
\num{5} (nenapu, 
gamana, \mo vugaLige) sigadiru; patetxyAgadiru; kANadiru; goVcaravAgadiru. 
\num{6} tapipxsiko; dUravAgiru; surakiSxtavAgiru; savxtaMtarxvAgiru: \eng{where
can we go to escape the crowds?} guMpiniMda dUravAgiralu nAvu elilxge 
hoVgabahudu?}}

\noindent 
\gl{\akirx}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (seremane, vayxkitx, \mo vugaLiMda) pArAgu; tapipxsiko; 
ODihoVgu; savxtaMtarxvAgu; biDugaDe hoMdu; vimoVcane paDe. 
\num{2} (anila, 
darxva yA kaNarUpada GanapadAthaRvu, pAterx, \mo vugaLiMda) soVru; soVrihoVgu;
horasUsu; horabaru. 
\num{3} surakiSxtavAgi --- pArAgu, tapipxsiko. 
\num{4} 
(ApAya, baMdhana, shikeSx, \mo vugaLiMda) tapipxsiko; (avugaLige) sigadiru.}

irisu; agalisu; beVreyAgisu: \eng{his profession as a travelling salesman has
estranged him from his family} avana saMcAriV mArATagArana vaqtitx avananunx 
saMsAradiMda dUra iriside.}

keSxVtarx.

\pron{yUkarisfTx}
\gl{\nA}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} yUkarisfTx; parxBuBoVjana; Esukirxsatxna aMtima rAtirx BoVjana.
\num{2} parxBuBoVjana AcaraNeyalilx baLasuva pavitarx vasutxgaLu, \kanmu\ berxDuDx matutx veYnu: \eng{give the Eucharist} yUkarisfTx parxsAda koDu, viniyoVgisu. 
\num{3} parxBuBoVjana saMsAkxra; berxDuDx, veYnugaLanunx aBimaMtirxsi sivxVkarisuva kerxYsatx matAcaraNe.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{Eucharistic}
\pron{yUkarisiTxkf}
\gl{\gu}
{\dictmeaning{yUkarisfTx AcaraNeya; parxBuBoVjana saMsAkxrakekx
saMbaMdhi\-sida.}} 

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{\eng{Eucharistic congress} yUkarisfTx samemxVLana; parxBuBoVjana samemxVLana; (modalige vASiRkavAgi naDeyutitxdudx, anaMtara devxYvASiRkavAgi naDeyutatx baMdiruva) kerxYsatxna (aMtima) rAtirxBoVjanada pavitarx AcaraNeya aMtararASiTxrXVya samemxVLana.}

\num{13} \eng{is he ever} (\ame, \ashi) avanu bahaLa: \eng{is he ever conceited} avanu bahaLa durahaMkAri. 
\num{14} \eng{yours ever} = \hyperlink{ever nuga9}{\nuga $(9)$}.}

\bentry
\word[excuse(1)]{excuse}
\pron{i(e)kfsxkUyxsfZ}
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (vayxkitxyanunx, kAyaRvanunx, tapapxnunx) maninxsu; kaSxmisu; kaSxmApaNemADu; mAphumADu. 
\num{2} (vayxkitxgAgi, tanagAgi, kataRvayx \mo vugaLiMda) biDugaDe paDe; vinAyiti paDe; tapipxsiko: \eng{asked the principal to excuse the boys from religious services} bAlakarige matiVya ArAdhanegaLiMda vinAyti koDabeVkeMdu pirxnisxpAlaranunx keVLidanu. 
\num{3} (vasutxgaLa \vi) (vayxkitxyanunx) nidoRVSiyeMdu toVrisu; niraparAdhiyeMdu toVrisu; tapupx mADilalxveMdu toVrisu. 
\num{4} (vasutxgaLa \vi) (kAyaR) tapipxlalxveMdu toVrisu; AparAdhavalalxveMdu toVrisu. 
\num{5} (vayxkitxyanunx yAvudeV kataRvayx \mo vugaLiMda) biDugaDe mADu; vinAyiti niVDu: \eng{he was excused from attending the meeting} avanige saBeya hAjarAtiyiMda vinAyiti dorakitu. 
\num{6} (salalx beVkAdudanunx, mADabeVkAdudanunx) otAtxya mADadiru; nibaRMdhisadiru; otAtxyisadiru; biTuTxkoDu: \eng{we will excuse your presence} niVvu barabeVkeMdu nAvu otAtxyisuvudilalx. \eng{we excuse the fee} rusumanunx biTuTxkoDutetxVve. 
\num{7} nevaheVLu; samathiRsiko; vivaraNe niVDu; samAdhAna heVLu; tapapxnunx pariharisikoLaLxlu parxyatinxsu: \eng{he excused his absence by saying that he was out of town} avanu baradidudxdakekx tAnu UralilxralilalxveMba neva heVLida. 
\num{8} nevavAgiru; samathaRne\-yAgiru; samAdhAnavAgiru; samathiRsu: \eng{ignorance of the law excuses no one from doing his duty} tananx kataRvayx neraveVrisadiruvudakekx kAnUnina

\bentry
\word{expect}
\pron{i(e)kfsxpekfTx}
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} edurunoVDu; niriVkiSxsu: \eng{I expect him to come} avanu barutAtxneMdu niriVkiSxsutitxdedxVne. 
\num{2} saMBavaveMdu BAvisu: \eng{I expect a storm} birumaLe saMBavaveMdu nAnaMdukoMDidedxVne. 
\num{3} salalxtakakxdeMdu niriVkiSxsu: \eng{do you expect payment for this?} idakekx haNa salalxtakakxdedxMdu niriVkiSxsutitxVyA? 
\num{4} (\AmA) aMduko; Uhisu; eNisu; BAvisu: \eng{I expect that they are on their way to war} avaru 
yudadxda hAdi hiDididAdxreMdu nAnu UhisutetxVne.}}

\noindent 
\gl{\nuga}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{be expecting a baby, a child, etc.} basirAgiru; gaBiRNiyAgiru. 
\num{2} \eng{expect me when you see me} (\AmA) nAnu yAvAga vApasAguvenoV tiLiyudu.

\num{6} (vAyxpitx, padada athaR, \mo vanunx) hecicxsuvudu; vishAlagoLisuvudu; visatxrisuvudu; visatxraNe. 
\num{7} (seVne) (sAlu \mo vugaLa \vi) samAMtara visatxraNe; seYnikara naDunaDuve samavAda aMtara biTuTx sAlanunx visatxrisuvudu yA seYnikara naDunaDuve samavAda aMtara biTuTx sAlu visAtxravAguvudu. 
\num{8} (\ashi) (kudare, jaTiTx ivara \vi) atiduDime; ati duDisuvudu; tiVra baLalisuvudu; susAtxguvaSuTx daNisuvudu; shakitxyanunx paramAvadhi baLasuvaMte balAtakxrisuvudu. 
\num{9} (keYyanunx, toVLanunx) niVDuvudu; cAcuvudu; niVDike; cAcike. 
\num{10} (daye, Asharxya) niVDike; dAna; parxdAna; niVDuvudu. 
\num{11} haravu; vAyxpitx; visAtxra.

\num{13} baDAvaNe; visatxraNa.

dUravANi.

\num{3} (AroVgayx, manoVBAvagaLu, \mo vugaLa \vi) ukikx hariyuva; tuMbi tuLukuva: \eng{exuberant love, health} tuMbituLukuva perxVma, AroVgayx. 
\num{4} (manuSayxru, kAyaRgaLu, \mo vugaLa \vi) utAsxhapUNaR; utAsxha tuMbida; suTiyAda; lavalavikeyuLaLx: \eng{an exuberant welcome for the hero} viVranige (niVDida) utAsxhaBarita sAvxgata.
